## TOPIC 01305: DAQmxReadDigitalU32

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__read__functions_1ga181bfa364ffe16a0cc0d38a0cd6bc85d.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__read__functions_1ga181bfa364ffe16a0cc0d38a0cd6bc85d.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxReadDigitalU32(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, float64 timeout, bool32 fillMode, uInt32 readArray[], uInt32 arraySizeInSamps, int32 *sampsPerChanRead, bool32 *reserved)RemarksReads multiple 32-bit integer samples from a task that contains one or more digital in

### DAQmxReadDigitalU32

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxReadDigitalU32(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, float64 timeout, bool32 fillMode, uInt32 readArray[], uInt32 arraySizeInSamps, int32 *sampsPerChanRead, bool32 *reserved)

#### Remarks

Reads multiple 32-bit integer samples from a task that contains one or more [digital input channels](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_virtchantypes). Use this function for devices with up to 32 lines per port. The samples are returned in unsigned [integer format](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_digitaldata).

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task to read samples from. |
| numSampsPerChan | [in] | int32 | The number of samples, per channel, to read. The default value of -1 (DAQmx_Val_Auto) reads all available samples. If readArray does not contain enough space, this function returns as many samples as fit in readArray. NI-DAQmx determines how many samples to read based on whether the task acquires samples continuously or acquires a finite number of samples. If the task acquires samples continuously and you set this parameter to -1, this function reads all the samples currently available in the buffer. If the task acquires a finite number of samples and you set this parameter to -1, the function waits for the task to acquire all requested samples, then reads those samples. If you set the Read All Available Samples property to TRUE, the function reads the samples currently available in the buffer and does not wait for the task to acquire all requested samples. |
| timeout | [in] | float64 | The amount of time, in seconds, to wait for the function to read the sample(s). To specify an infinite wait, pass -1 (DAQmx_Val_WaitInfinitely). This function returns an error if the timeout elapses. A value of 0 indicates to try once to read the requested samples. If all the requested samples are read, the function is successful. Otherwise, the function returns a timeout error and returns the samples that were actually read. |
| fillMode | [in] | bool32 | Specifies whether or not the samples are interleaved. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_GroupByChannelGroup by channel (non-interleaved)DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumberGroup by scan number (interleaved) |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByChannel | Group by channel (non-interleaved) |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumber | Group by scan number (interleaved) |  |  |
| arraySizeInSamps | [in] | uInt32 | The size of the array, in samples, into which samples are read. |
| reserved | [in] | bool32 * | Reserved for future use. Pass NULL to this parameter. |
| readArray | [out] | uInt32[] | The array to read samples into, organized according to fillMode. |
| sampsPerChanRead | [out] | int32 * | The actual number of samples read from each channel. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

Read Functions

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-c-api-ref path=group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__read__functions_1ga198145831f03d8635d749901aab88331.html language=enus -->

### DAQmxReadCtrFreq

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxReadCtrFreq(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, float64 timeout, bool32 interleaved, float64 readArrayFrequency[], float64 readArrayDutyCycle[], uInt32 arraySizeInSamps, int32 *sampsPerChanRead, bool32 *reserved)

#### Remarks

Reads one or more pairs of pulse frequency and duty cycle from a counter input task.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task to read samples from. |
| numSampsPerChan | [in] | int32 | The number of samples, per channel, to read. The default value of -1 (DAQmx_Val_Auto) reads all available samples. If readArray does not contain enough space, this function returns as many samples as fit in readArray. NI-DAQmx determines how many samples to read based on whether the task acquires samples continuously or acquires a finite number of samples. If the task acquires samples continuously and you set this parameter to -1, this function reads all the samples currently available in the buffer. If the task acquires a finite number of samples and you set this parameter to -1, the function waits for the task to acquire all requested samples, then reads those samples. If you set the Read All Available Samples property to TRUE, the function reads the samples currently available in the buffer and does not wait for the task to acquire all requested samples. |
| timeout | [in] | float64 | The amount of time, in seconds, to wait for the function to read the sample(s). To specify an infinite wait, pass -1 (DAQmx_Val_WaitInfinitely). This function returns an error if the timeout elapses. A value of 0 indicates to try once to read the requested samples. If all the requested samples are read, the function is successful. Otherwise, the function returns a timeout error and returns the samples that were actually read. |
| interleaved | [in] | bool32 | Specifies whether or not the samples are interleaved. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_GroupByChannelGroup by channel (non-interleaved)DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumberGroup by scan number (interleaved) |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByChannel | Group by channel (non-interleaved) |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumber | Group by scan number (interleaved) |  |  |
| arraySizeInSamps | [in] | uInt32 | The size of the array, in samples, into which samples are read. |
| reserved | [in] | bool32 * | Reserved for future use. Pass NULL to this parameter. |
| readArrayFrequency | [out] | float64[] | The array to read frequency samples into. |
| readArrayDutyCycle | [out] | float64[] | The array to read duty cycles into. The duty cycle is the pulse high time divided by the pulse period. |
| sampsPerChanRead | [out] | int32 * | The actual number of samples read from each channel. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

## TOPIC 01309: DAQmxReadCounterU32Ex

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__read__functions_1ga4958130625ba30c40ffef432ffa8d7a2.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__read__functions_1ga4958130625ba30c40ffef432ffa8d7a2.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxReadCounterU32Ex(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, float64 timeout, bool32 fillMode, uInt32 readArray[], uInt32 arraySizeInSamps, int32 *sampsPerChanRead, bool32 *reserved)RemarksReads multiple 32-bit integer samples from a counter task. Use this function when co

### DAQmxReadCounterU32Ex

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxReadCounterU32Ex(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, float64 timeout, bool32 fillMode, uInt32 readArray[], uInt32 arraySizeInSamps, int32 *sampsPerChanRead, bool32 *reserved)

#### Remarks

Reads multiple 32-bit integer samples from a counter task. Use this function when counter samples are returned unscaled, such as for edge counting.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task to read samples from. |
| numSampsPerChan | [in] | int32 | The number of samples, per channel, to read. The default value of -1 (DAQmx_Val_Auto) reads all available samples. If readArray does not contain enough space, this function returns as many samples as fit in readArray. NI-DAQmx determines how many samples to read based on whether the task acquires samples continuously or acquires a finite number of samples. If the task acquires samples continuously and you set this parameter to -1, this function reads all the samples currently available in the buffer. If the task acquires a finite number of samples and you set this parameter to -1, the function waits for the task to acquire all requested samples, then reads those samples. If you set the Read All Available Samples property to TRUE, the function reads the samples currently available in the buffer and does not wait for the task to acquire all requested samples. |
| timeout | [in] | float64 | The amount of time, in seconds, to wait for the function to read the sample(s). To specify an infinite wait, pass -1 (DAQmx_Val_WaitInfinitely). This function returns an error if the timeout elapses. A value of 0 indicates to try once to read the requested samples. If all the requested samples are read, the function is successful. Otherwise, the function returns a timeout error and returns the samples that were actually read. |
| fillMode | [in] | bool32 | Specifies whether or not the samples are interleaved. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_GroupByChannelGroup by channel (non-interleaved)DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumberGroup by scan number (interleaved) |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByChannel | Group by channel (non-interleaved) |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumber | Group by scan number (interleaved) |  |  |
| arraySizeInSamps | [in] | uInt32 | The size of the array, in samples, into which samples are read. |
| reserved | [in] | bool32 * | Reserved for future use. Pass NULL to this parameter. |
| readArray | [out] | uInt32[] | The array to read samples into. |
| sampsPerChanRead | [out] | int32 * | The actual number of samples read from each channel. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

## TOPIC 01310: DAQmxReadCtrTicks

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__read__functions_1ga515c568dc19831d0e3b75a22b68b0e40.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__read__functions_1ga515c568dc19831d0e3b75a22b68b0e40.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxReadCtrTicks(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, float64 timeout, bool32 interleaved, uInt32 readArrayHighTicks[], uInt32 readArrayLowTicks[], uInt32 arraySizeInSamps, int32 *sampsPerChanRead, bool32 *reserved)RemarksReads one or more pairs of pulse high and low ti

### DAQmxReadCtrTicks

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxReadCtrTicks(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, float64 timeout, bool32 interleaved, uInt32 readArrayHighTicks[], uInt32 readArrayLowTicks[], uInt32 arraySizeInSamps, int32 *sampsPerChanRead, bool32 *reserved)

#### Remarks

Reads one or more pairs of pulse high and low tick counts from a counter input task.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task to read samples from. |
| numSampsPerChan | [in] | int32 | The number of samples, per channel, to read. The default value of -1 (DAQmx_Val_Auto) reads all available samples. If readArray does not contain enough space, this function returns as many samples as fit in readArray. NI-DAQmx determines how many samples to read based on whether the task acquires samples continuously or acquires a finite number of samples. If the task acquires samples continuously and you set this parameter to -1, this function reads all the samples currently available in the buffer. If the task acquires a finite number of samples and you set this parameter to -1, the function waits for the task to acquire all requested samples, then reads those samples. If you set the Read All Available Samples property to TRUE, the function reads the samples currently available in the buffer and does not wait for the task to acquire all requested samples. |
| timeout | [in] | float64 | The amount of time, in seconds, to wait for the function to read the sample(s). To specify an infinite wait, pass -1 (DAQmx_Val_WaitInfinitely). This function returns an error if the timeout elapses. A value of 0 indicates to try once to read the requested samples. If all the requested samples are read, the function is successful. Otherwise, the function returns a timeout error and returns the samples that were actually read. |
| interleaved | [in] | bool32 | Specifies whether or not the samples are interleaved. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_GroupByChannelGroup by channel (non-interleaved)DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumberGroup by scan number (interleaved) |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByChannel | Group by channel (non-interleaved) |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumber | Group by scan number (interleaved) |  |  |
| arraySizeInSamps | [in] | uInt32 | The size of the array, in samples, into which samples are read. |
| reserved | [in] | bool32 * | Reserved for future use. Pass NULL to this parameter. |
| readArrayHighTicks | [out] | uInt32[] | The array to read the number of high ticks into. |
| readArrayLowTicks | [out] | uInt32[] | The array to read the number of low ticks into. |
| sampsPerChanRead | [out] | int32 * | The actual number of samples read from each channel. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

Otherwise, the function returns a timeout error and returns the samples that were actually read. |

| value | [out] | float64 * | The sample read from the task. |

If the task acquires samples continuously and you set this parameter to -1, this function reads all the samples currently available in the buffer. If the task acquires a finite number of samples and you set this parameter to -1, the function waits for the task to acquire all requested samples, then reads those samples. If you set the Read All Available Samples property to TRUE, the function reads the samples currently available in the buffer and does not wait for the task to acquire all requested samples. |
| timeout | [in] | float64 | The amount of time, in seconds, to wait for the function to read the sample(s). To specify an infinite wait, pass -1 (DAQmx_Val_WaitInfinitely). This function returns an error if the timeout elapses. A value of 0 indicates to try once to read the requested samples. If all the requested samples are read, the function is successful. Otherwise, the function returns a timeout error and returns the samples that were actually read. |

Reads one or more [unscaled](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_unscaleddata) 32-bit signed integer samples from a task that contains one or more [analog input channels](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_virtchantypes).

If the task acquires a finite number of samples and you set this parameter to -1, the function waits for the task to acquire all requested samples, then reads those samples. Each

### DAQmxReadDigitalLines

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxReadDigitalLines(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, float64 timeout, bool32 fillMode, uInt8 readArray[], uInt32 arraySizeInBytes, int32 *sampsPerChanRead, int32 *numBytesPerSamp, bool32 *reserved)

#### Remarks

Reads multiple samples from each digital line in a task. Each line in a channel gets one byte per sample.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task to read samples from. |
| numSampsPerChan | [in] | int32 | The number of samples, per channel, to read. The default value of -1 (DAQmx_Val_Auto) reads all available samples. If readArray does not contain enough space, this function returns as many samples as fit in readArray. NI-DAQmx determines how many samples to read based on whether the task acquires samples continuously or acquires a finite number of samples. If the task acquires samples continuously and you set this parameter to -1, this function reads all the samples currently available in the buffer. If the task acquires a finite number of samples and you set this parameter to -1, the function waits for the task to acquire all requested samples, then reads those samples. If you set the Read All Available Data property to TRUE, the function reads the samples currently available in the buffer and does not wait for the task to acquire all requested samples. |
| timeout | [in] | float64 | The amount of time, in seconds, to wait for the function to read the sample(s). To specify an infinite wait, pass -1 (DAQmx_Val_WaitInfinitely). This function returns an error if the timeout elapses. A value of 0 indicates to try once to read the requested samples. If all the requested samples are read, the function is successful. Otherwise, the function returns a timeout error and returns the samples that were actually read. |
| fillMode | [in] | bool32 | Specifies whether or not the samples are interleaved. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_GroupByChannelGroup by channel (non-interleaved)DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumberGroup by scan number (interleaved) |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByChannel | Group by channel (non-interleaved) |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumber | Group by scan number (interleaved) |  |  |
| arraySizeInBytes | [in] | uInt32 | The size of the array, in samples, into which samples are read. |
| reserved | [in] | bool32 * | Reserved for future use. Pass NULL to this parameter. |
| readArray | [out] | uInt8[] | The array to read samples into. Each numBytesPerSamp corresponds to one sample per channel, with each element in that grouping corresponding to a line in that channel, up to the number of lines contained in the channel. |
| sampsPerChanRead | [out] | int32 * | The actual number of samples read from each channel. |
| numBytesPerSamp | [out] | int32 * | The number of elements in readArray that constitutes a sample per channel. For each sample per channel, numBytesPerSamp is the number of bytes that channel consists of. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

### DAQmxReadCtrFreqScalar

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxReadCtrFreqScalar(TaskHandle taskHandle, float64 timeout, float64 *frequency, float64 *dutyCycle, bool32 *reserved)

#### Remarks

Reads a single pair of pulse frequency and duty cycle from a counter input task.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task to read the sample from. |
| timeout | [in] | float64 | The amount of time, in seconds, to wait for the function to read the sample(s). To specify an infinite wait, pass -1 (DAQmx_Val_WaitInfinitely). This function returns an error if the timeout elapses. A value of 0 indicates to try once to read the requested samples. If all the requested samples are read, the function is successful. Otherwise, the function returns a timeout error and returns the samples that were actually read. |
| reserved | [in] | bool32 * | Reserved for future use. Pass NULL to this parameter. |
| frequency | [out] | float64 * | The pulse frequency. |
| dutyCycle | [out] | float64 * | The pulse high time divided by the pulse period. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

## TOPIC 01319: DAQmxReadDigitalScalarU32

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`

- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxReadDigitalScalarU32(TaskHandle taskHandle, float64 timeout, uInt32 *value, bool32 *reserved)RemarksReads a single 32-bit integer sample from a task that contains a single digital input channel. Use this function for devices with up to 32 lines per port. The sample is return

### DAQmxReadDigitalScalarU32

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxReadDigitalScalarU32(TaskHandle taskHandle, float64 timeout, uInt32 *value, bool32 *reserved)

#### Remarks

Reads a single 32-bit integer sample from a task that contains a single [digital input channel](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_virtchantypes). Use this function for devices with up to 32 lines per port. The sample is returned in unsigned [integer format](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_digitaldata).

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task to read the sample from. |
| timeout | [in] | float64 | The amount of time, in seconds, to wait for the function to read the sample. The default value is 10.0 seconds. To specify an infinite wait, pass -1 (DAQmx_Val_WaitInfinitely). This function returns an error if the timeout elapses. A value of 0 indicates to try once to read the requested sample. If the entire requested sample is read, the function is successful. Otherwise, the function returns a timeout error and returns what was actually read. |
| reserved | [in] | bool32 * | Reserved for future use. Pass NULL to this parameter. |
| value | [out] | uInt32 * | The sample read from the task. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 01320: DAQmxReadCounterF64

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__read__functions_1gaf2ab9ad7ec64ab0f3d1158814ea358c2.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__read__functions_1gaf2ab9ad7ec64ab0f3d1158814ea358c2.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxReadCounterF64(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, float64 timeout, float64 readArray[], uInt32 arraySizeInSamps, int32 *sampsPerChanRead, bool32 *reserved)RemarksReads multiple floating-point samples from a counter task. Use this function when counter samples are

### DAQmxReadCounterF64

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxReadCounterF64(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, float64 timeout, float64 readArray[], uInt32 arraySizeInSamps, int32 *sampsPerChanRead, bool32 *reserved)

#### Remarks

Reads multiple floating-point samples from a counter task. Use this function when counter samples are interleaved, and are scaled to a floating-point value, such as for frequency and period measurements.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task to read samples from. |
| numSampsPerChan | [in] | int32 | The number of samples, per channel, to read. The default value of -1 (DAQmx_Val_Auto) reads all available samples. If readArray does not contain enough space, this function returns as many samples as fit in readArray. NI-DAQmx determines how many samples to read based on whether the task acquires samples continuously or acquires a finite number of samples. If the task acquires samples continuously and you set this parameter to -1, this function reads all the samples currently available in the buffer. If the task acquires a finite number of samples and you set this parameter to -1, the function waits for the task to acquire all requested samples, then reads those samples. If you set the Read All Available Samples property to TRUE, the function reads the samples currently available in the buffer and does not wait for the task to acquire all requested samples. |
| timeout | [in] | float64 | The amount of time, in seconds, to wait for the function to read the sample(s). To specify an infinite wait, pass -1 (DAQmx_Val_WaitInfinitely). This function returns an error if the timeout elapses. A value of 0 indicates to try once to read the requested samples. If all the requested samples are read, the function is successful. Otherwise, the function returns a timeout error and returns the samples that were actually read. |
| arraySizeInSamps | [in] | uInt32 | The size of the array, in samples, into which samples are read. |
| reserved | [in] | bool32 * | Reserved for future use. Pass NULL to this parameter. |
| readArray | [out] | float64[] | The array to read samples into. |
| sampsPerChanRead | [out] | int32 * | The actual number of samples read from each channel. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

Read Functions

### DAQmxReadBinaryU32

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxReadBinaryU32(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, float64 timeout, bool32 fillMode, uInt32 readArray[], uInt32 arraySizeInSamps, int32 *sampsPerChanRead, bool32 *reserved)

#### Remarks

Reads one or more [unscaled](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_unscaleddata) 32-bit unsigned integer samples from a task that contains one or more [analog input channels](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_virtchantypes).

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task used in this function. |
| numSampsPerChan | [in] | int32 | The number of samples, per channel, to read. The default value of -1 (DAQmx_Val_Auto) reads all available samples. If readArray does not contain enough space, this function returns as many samples as fit in readArray. NI-DAQmx determines how many samples to read based on whether the task acquires samples continuously or acquires a finite number of samples. If the task acquires samples continuously and you set this parameter to -1, this function reads all the samples currently available in the buffer. If the task acquires a finite number of samples and you set this parameter to -1, the function waits for the task to acquire all requested samples, then reads those samples. If you set the Read All Available Samples property to TRUE, the function reads the samples currently available in the buffer and does not wait for the task to acquire all requested samples. |
| timeout | [in] | float64 | The amount of time, in seconds, to wait for the function to read the sample(s). To specify an infinite wait, pass -1 (DAQmx_Val_WaitInfinitely). This function returns an error if the timeout elapses. A value of 0 indicates to try once to read the requested samples. If all the requested samples are read, the function is successful. Otherwise, the function returns a timeout error and returns the samples that were actually read. |
| fillMode | [in] | bool32 | Specifies whether or not the samples are interleaved. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_GroupByChannelGroup by channel (non-interleaved)DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumberGroup by scan number (interleaved) |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByChannel | Group by channel (non-interleaved) |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumber | Group by scan number (interleaved) |  |  |
| arraySizeInSamps | [in] | uInt32 | The size of the array, in samples, into which samples are read. |
| reserved | [in] | bool32 * | Reserved for future use. Pass NULL to this parameter. |
| readArray | [out] | uInt32[] | The array to read samples into, organized according to fillMode. |
| sampsPerChanRead | [out] | int32 * | The actual number of samples read from each channel. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`

- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxGetNthTaskReadChannel(TaskHandle taskHandle, uInt32 index, char buffer[], int32 bufferSize)RemarksReturns the Nth channel of the channels that are configured to be read by the DAQmxSetReadChannelsToRead property. This function takes the taskHandle, index, and bufferSize you

### DAQmxGetNthTaskReadChannel

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxGetNthTaskReadChannel(TaskHandle taskHandle, uInt32 index, char buffer[], int32 bufferSize)

#### Remarks

Returns the Nth channel of the channels that are configured to be read by the [DAQmxSetReadChannelsToRead](group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__read_1gad338eaacc8e88435cf18727f4562bb7f.html) property. This function takes the taskHandle, index, and bufferSize you specify and returns the Nth channel.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task used in this function. |
| index | [in] | uInt32 | The _N_th channel to return. The index starts at 1. |
| bufferSize | [in] | int32 | The size, in bytes, of buffer. If you pass 0, this function returns the number of bytes needed to allocate. |
| buffer | [out] | char[] | The _N_th channel in the index. If you pass NULL, this function returns the number of bytes needed to allocate. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A negative value indicates an error. For this function, if you pass NULL for the buffer or 0 for the buffer size, this function returns the number of bytes needed to allocate.

## TOPIC 01325: DAQmxReadRaw

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__read__functions__advanced_1gac08799316f0dfab9f1d792d0f27902eb.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__read__functions__advanced_1gac08799316f0dfab9f1d792d0f27902eb.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxReadRaw(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, float64 timeout, void *readArray, uInt32 arraySizeInBytes, int32 *sampsRead, int32 *numBytesPerSamp, bool32 *reserved)RemarksReads raw samples directly from the input lines. There is no scaling, parsing, or separation of

### DAQmxReadRaw

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxReadRaw(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, float64 timeout, void *readArray, uInt32 arraySizeInBytes, int32 *sampsRead, int32 *numBytesPerSamp, bool32 *reserved)

#### Remarks

Reads [raw](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_rawdata) samples directly from the input lines. There is no scaling, parsing, or separation of the samples. Refer to the specifications for your device to determine the format of the incoming samples.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task to read samples from. |
| numSampsPerChan | [in] | int32 | The number of samples, per channel, to read. If you set this parameter to -1 (DAQmx_Val_Auto), NI-DAQmx determines how many samples to read based on whether the task acquires samples continuously or acquires a finite number of samples. If the task acquires samples continuously and you set this parameter to -1, this function reads all the samples currently available in the buffer. If readArray does not contain enough space, this function returns as many samples as fit in readArray. If the task acquires a finite number of samples and you set this parameter to -1, the function waits for the task to acquire all requested samples, then reads those samples. If you set the Read All Available Data property to TRUE, the function reads the samples currently available in the buffer and does not wait for the task to acquire all requested samples. |
| timeout | [in] | float64 | The amount of time, in seconds, to wait for the function to read the sample(s). To specify an infinite wait, pass -1 (DAQmx_Val_WaitInfinitely). This function returns an error if the timeout elapses. A value of 0 indicates to try once to read the requested samples. If all the requested samples are read, the function is successful. Otherwise, the function returns a timeout error and returns the samples that were actually read. |
| arraySizeInBytes | [in] | uInt32 | The size of the array into which samples are read. |
| reserved | [in] | bool32 * | Reserved for future use. Pass NULL to this parameter. |
| readArray | [out] | void * | The array into which samples are read. |
| sampsRead | [out] | int32 * | The actual number of samples read into the array per scan. |
| numBytesPerSamp | [out] | int32 * | The number of elements in readArray that constitutes a sample. This value takes into account all channels that are read. For example, five channels giving 12 bytes for one entire scan return 12 bytes. The value is not divided along channel lines. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

Advanced

## TOPIC 01327: DAQmxCreatePolynomialScale

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__scale__configuration_1ga02b903228520810a4aabd934296cb19c.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__scale__configuration_1ga02b903228520810a4aabd934296cb19c.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxCreatePolynomialScale(const char name[], const float64 forwardCoeffs[], uInt32 numForwardCoeffsIn, const float64 reverseCoeffs[], uInt32 numReverseCoeffsIn, int32 preScaledUnits, const char scaledUnits[])RemarksCreates and configures a scale that uses an nth order polynomial

### DAQmxCreatePolynomialScale

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxCreatePolynomialScale(const char name[], const float64 forwardCoeffs[], uInt32 numForwardCoeffsIn, const float64 reverseCoeffs[], uInt32 numReverseCoeffsIn, int32 preScaledUnits, const char scaledUnits[])

#### Remarks

Creates and configures a scale that uses an nth order polynomial equation. NI-DAQmx requires both a polynomial to convert prescaled values to scaled values (forward) and a polynomial to convert scaled values to prescaled values (reverse). If you know only one set of coefficients, use [DAQmxCalculateReversePolyCoeff](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__scale__configuration_1ga09d15d5045ea859339545904559d95de.html) to generate the other set.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| name | [in] | const char[] | Identifies the custom scale for later use, such as when you create channels. |
| forwardCoeffs | [in] | const float64[] | An array of coefficients for the polynomial that converts prescaled values to scaled values. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. For example, if index 3 of the array is 9, the fourth term of the equation is 9x3. |
| numForwardCoeffsIn | [in] | uInt32 | The number of elements in forwardCoeff. |
| reverseCoeffs | [in] | const float64[] | An array of coefficients for the polynomial that converts scaled values to prescaled values. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. For example, if index 3 of the array is 9, the fourth term of the equation is 9y3. |
| numReverseCoeffsIn | [in] | uInt32 | The number of elements in reverseCoeff. |
| preScaledUnits | [in] | int32 | The units of the values to scale. ## TOPIC 01328: DAQmxCalculateReversePolyCoeff

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__scale__configuration_1ga09d15d5045ea859339545904559d95de.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__scale__configuration_1ga09d15d5045ea859339545904559d95de.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxCalculateReversePolyCoeff(const float64 forwardCoeffs[], uInt32 numForwardCoeffsIn, float64 minValX, float64 maxValX, int32 numPointsToCompute, int32 reversePolyOrder, float64 reverseCoeffs[])RemarksComputes a set of coefficients for a polynomial that approximates the invers

### DAQmxCalculateReversePolyCoeff

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxCalculateReversePolyCoeff(const float64 forwardCoeffs[], uInt32 numForwardCoeffsIn, float64 minValX, float64 maxValX, int32 numPointsToCompute, int32 reversePolyOrder, float64 reverseCoeffs[])

#### Remarks

Computes a set of coefficients for a polynomial that approximates the inverse of the polynomial with the coefficients you specify with forwardCoeffs. The function generates a table of x versus y values over the range of x. The function then finds a polynomial fit, using the least squares method to compute a polynomial that computes an x given a y.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| forwardCoeffs | [in] | const float64[] | The array of the forward coefficients for the polynomial that computes y given a value of x. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. For example, if index 3 of the array is 9, the fourth term of the equation is 9x3. |
| numForwardCoeffsIn | [in] | uInt32 | The number of elements in forwardCoeff. |
| minValX | [in] | float64 | The minimum value of x for which you use the polynomial. This is the smallest value of x for which the function generates a y value in the table. |
| maxValX | [in] | float64 | The maximum value of x for which you use the polynomial. This is the largest value of x for which the function generates a y value in the table. |
| numPointsToCompute | [in] | int32 | The number of points in the table of x versus y values. The function spaces the values evenly between minValX and maxValX. |
| reversePolyOrder | [in] | int32 | The order of the reverse polynomial to compute. For example, an input of 3 indicates a 3rd order polynomial. An input of -1 indicates to compute a reverse polynomial of the same order as the forward polynomial. |
| reverseCoeffs | [out] | float64[] | The array of the reverse coefficients of the polynomial. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. For example, if index 3 of the array is 9, the fourth term of the equation is 9y3. reverseCoeffs will be one greater than what you passed for reversePolyOrder. If you pass -1 for reversePolyOrder, the array must be the size of forwardCoeffs. Otherwise, the behavior is undefined. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

Scale Configuration

### DAQmxCreateLinScale

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxCreateLinScale(const char name[], float64 slope, float64 yIntercept, int32 preScaledUnits, const char scaledUnits[])

#### Remarks

Creates and configures a scale that uses the equation y=mx+b, where x is the prescaled value and y is the scaled value. The equation is identical for input and output. If your equation is in the form x=my+b, you must first solve for y in terms of x.

| preScaledUnits | [in] | int32 | The units of the values to scale. ## TOPIC 01332: DAQmxSetDigitalPowerUpStatesEx

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__system__configuration_1ga2ca7bb4279e581c3c0ff3dc50438a809.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__system__configuration_1ga2ca7bb4279e581c3c0ff3dc50438a809.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxSetDigitalPowerUpStatesEx(const char channelNames[], const int32 stateArray[], uInt32 arraySize)RemarksUpdates the state that digital physical channels on static DIO devices are set to when the device powers up or when the device is reset. Power-up states are stored in EEPRO

### DAQmxSetDigitalPowerUpStatesEx

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxSetDigitalPowerUpStatesEx(const char channelNames[], const int32 stateArray[], uInt32 arraySize)

#### Remarks

Updates the state that digital physical channels on static DIO devices are set to when the device powers up or when the device is reset. Power-up states are stored in EEPROMs that you can write to only a limited number of times. Therefore, you should use this function as infrequently as possible. This function writes to the EEPROM only if a setting you request is different from the one currently stored on the EEPROM. This function writes power-up states in sequential order. Therefore, if a physical channel has multiple entries, the last entry is used.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| channelNames | [in] | const char[] | The digital lines or ports to modify. You cannot set power-up states for dedicated digital input lines. You can specify a list or range of channels. |
| stateArray | [in] | const int32[] | The power-up states to set for the channels in channelNames. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_HighHigh logicDAQmx_Val_LowLow logicDAQmx_Val_TristateHigh-impedance state. You can select this state only on devices with bidirectional ports, and you can select it only for entire ports. You cannot select this state for dedicated digital output lines. |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_High | High logic |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Low | Low logic |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Tristate | High-impedance state. You can select this state only on devices with bidirectional ports, and you can select it only for entire ports. You cannot select this state for dedicated digital output lines. |  |  |
| arraySize | [in] | uInt32 | The number of power-up states in stateArray. This must be equal to the number of channels in channelNames. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

System Configuration

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-c-api-ref path=group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__system__configuration_1ga31dc423cc93dc0cb3bb52354b00eb3d1.html language=enus -->

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`

### DAQmxReadIDPinMemory

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxReadIDPinMemory(const char deviceName[], const char idPinName[], uInt8 data[], uInt32 arraySize, uInt32 *dataLengthRead, uInt32 *formatCode)

#### Remarks

Reads and returns the data and Format Code stored in the memory attached to the specified ID Pin.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| deviceName |  | const char[] | Specifies the name to assign to the device. If unspecified, NI-DAQmx chooses the device name. |
| idPinName |  | const char[] | Specifies the name of ID Pin to perform operation on. |
| data |  | uInt8[] | The array to store the data read from the memory into. |
| arraySize |  | uInt32 | The size of the array into which the data is read. |
| dataLengthRead |  | uInt32 * | The actual size of the data read in bytes. |
| formatCode |  | uInt32 * | The Format Code indicating the type and structure of the data. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

## TOPIC 01334: DAQmxGetDigitalPullUpPullDownStates

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`

- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC_C DAQmxGetDigitalPullUpPullDownStates(const char deviceName[], const char channelName[], int32 *state,...)RemarksGets the resistor level for lines when they are in tristate logic.ParametersNameDirectionTypeDescriptiondeviceName[in]const char[]Specifies the name to assign to the d

### DAQmxGetDigitalPullUpPullDownStates

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC_C DAQmxGetDigitalPullUpPullDownStates(const char deviceName[], const char channelName[], int32 *state,...)

#### Remarks

Gets the resistor level for lines when they are in tristate logic.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| deviceName | [in] | const char[] | Specifies the name to assign to the device. If unspecified, NI-DAQmx chooses the device name. |
| channelName | [in] | const char[] | The digital line or port to get the power-up state from. You can specify a list or range of channels. |
| state | [out] | int32 * | The power-up state for the channel in channelName. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_PullUpHigh logicDAQmx_Val_PullDownLow logic |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_PullUp | High logic |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_PullDown | Low logic |  |  |
| ... | [out] | - | Pairs of additional channels and the states to get when the device powers up or when the device is reset. You must pass NULL at the end of the argument list. If you do not want to pass additional channels and states, the function call can be similar to the following example: DAQmxGetDigitalPullUpPullDownStates ("Dev1", "Dev1/do0", &state, NULL); If you pass additional channels and states, the function call can be similar to the following example: DAQmxGetDigitalPullUpPullDownStates ("Dev1", "Dev1/do0", &state_do0, "Dev1/do1", &state_do1, NULL); |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

If unspecified

### DAQmxGetDigitalPowerUpStates

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC_C DAQmxGetDigitalPowerUpStates(const char deviceName[], const char channelName[], int32 *state,...)

#### Remarks

Gets the power-up states for digital physical lines.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| deviceName | [in] | const char[] | Specifies the name to assign to the device. If unspecified, NI-DAQmx chooses the device name. |
| channelName | [in] | const char[] | The digital line or port to get the power-up state from. You can specify a list or range of channels. |
| state | [out] | int32 * | The power-up state for the channel in channelName. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_HighHigh logicDAQmx_Val_LowLow logicDAQmx_Val_TristateHigh-impedance state. You can select this state only on devices with bidirectional ports, and you can select it only for entire ports. You cannot select this state for dedicated digital output lines. |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_High | High logic |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Low | Low logic |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Tristate | High-impedance state. You can select this state only on devices with bidirectional ports, and you can select it only for entire ports. You cannot select this state for dedicated digital output lines. |  |  |
| ... | [out] | - | Pairs of additional channels and the states to get when the device powers up or when the device is reset. You must pass NULL at the end of the argument list. If you do not want to pass additional channels and states, the function call can be similar to the following example: DAQmxGetDigitalPowerUpStates ("Dev1", "Dev1/do0", &state, NULL); If you pass additional channels and states, the function call can be similar to the following example: DAQmxGetDigitalPowerUpStates ("Dev1", "Dev1/do0", &state_do0, "Dev1/do1", &state_do1, NULL); |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

### DAQmxGetAnalogPowerUpStates

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC_C DAQmxGetAnalogPowerUpStates(const char deviceName[], const char channelName[], float64 *state, int32 channelType,...)

#### Remarks

Gets the power-up states for analog physical channels. (Windows) This function is deprecated. Use the [DAQmxGetAnalogPowerUpStatesWithOutputType](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__system__configuration_1gac76c8c955a7af119935602da8d9b7272.html) function instead. National Instruments recommends that you avoid using deprecated functions. These functions may become obsolete in future releases. (Linux) This function is not supported on Linux.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| deviceName | [in] | const char[] | Specifies the name to assign to the device. If unspecified, NI-DAQmx chooses the device name. |
| channelName | [in] | const char[] | The physical channel to get the power-up state from. You can specify a list or range of channels. |
| state | [out] | float64 * | The power-up state for the channel in channelName. |
| channelType | [out] | int32 | The channel type for the channel in channelName. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_ChannelVoltageVoltageDAQmx_Val_ChannelCurrentCurrent |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_ChannelVoltage | Voltage |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_ChannelCurrent | Current |  |  |
| ... | [out] | - | Pairs of additional channels and the states to get when the device powers up or when the device is reset. You must pass NULL at the end of the argument list. If you do not want to pass additional channels and states, the function call can be similar to the following example: DAQmxGetAnalogPowerUpStates ("Dev1", "Dev1/ao0", &state, DAQmx_Val_ChannelVoltage, NULL); If you pass additional channels and states, the function call can be similar to the following example: DAQmxGetAnalogPowerUpStates ("Dev1", "Dev1/ao0", &state_ao0, DAQmx_Val_ChannelVoltage, "Dev1/ao1", &state_ao1, DAQmx_Val_ChannelCurrent, NULL); |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

### DAQmxConfigureLogging

| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task used in this function. |
| filePath | [in] | const char[] | The path to the TDMS file to which you want to log data. |
| loggingMode | [in] | int32 | Specifies whether to enable logging and whether to allow reading data while logging. Log mode allows for the best performance. However, you cannot read data while logging if you specify this mode. If you want to read data while logging, specify Log and Read mode. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_OffDisable logging for the task.DAQmx_Val_LogEnable logging for the task. You cannot read data using DAQmx Read when using this mode. If you require access to the data, read from the TDMS file.DAQmx_Val_LogAndReadEnable both logging and reading data for the task. You must use DAQmx Read to read samples for NI-DAQmx to stream them to disk. |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Off | Disable logging for the task. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Log | Enable logging for the task. You cannot read data using DAQmx Read when using this mode. If you require access to the data, read from the TDMS file. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_LogAndRead | Enable both logging and reading data for the task. You must use DAQmx Read to read samples for NI-DAQmx to stream them to disk. |  |  |
| groupName | [in] | const char[] | The name of the group to create within the TDMS file for data from this task. If you append data to an existing file and the specified group already exists, NI-DAQmx appends a number symbol and a number to the group name, incrementing that number until finding a group name that does not exist. For example, if you specify a group name of Voltage Task, and that group already exists, NI-DAQmx assigns the group name Voltage Task #1, then Voltage Task #2. If you do not specify a group name, NI-DAQmx uses the name of the task. For digital input tasks, NI-DAQmx creates a group for each virtual channel in the task. For each created group, NI-DAQmx appends a hyphen and the virtual channel name to the group name. |
| operation | [in] | int32 | Specifies how to open the TDMS file. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_OpenOpen an existing TDMS file, and append data to that file. If the file does not exist, NI-DAQmx returns an error.DAQmx_Val_OpenOrCreateOpen an existing TDMS file, and append data to that file. If the file does not exist, NI-DAQmx creates a new TDMS file.DAQmx_Val_CreateOrReplaceCreate a new TDMS file, or replace an existing TDMS file.DAQmx_Val_CreateCreate a new TDMS file. If the file already exists, NI-DAQmx returns an error. |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Open | Open an existing TDMS file, and append data to that file. If the file does not exist, NI-DAQmx returns an error. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_OpenOrCreate | Open an existing TDMS file, and append data to that file. If the file does not exist, NI-DAQmx creates a new TDMS file. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_CreateOrReplace | Create a new TDMS file, or replace an existing TDMS file. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Create | Create a new TDMS file. If the file already exists, NI-DAQmx returns an error. |  |  |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

## TOPIC 01345: DAQmxStopTask

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__task__configuration__control_1ga85d6ee7f3518c1eb26ec0f01de160392.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__task__configuration__control_1ga85d6ee7f3518c1eb26ec0f01de160392.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxStopTask(TaskHandle taskHandle)RemarksStops the task and returns it to the state it was in before you called DAQmxStartTask or called an NI-DAQmx Write function with autoStart set to TRUE. If you do not call DAQmxStartTask and DAQmxStopTask when you call NI-DAQmx Read functi

### DAQmxStopTask

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxStopTask(TaskHandle taskHandle)

#### Remarks

Stops the [task](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_tasksnidaqmx) and returns it to the [state](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_taskstatemodel) it was in before you called DAQmxStartTask or called an NI-DAQmx Write function with autoStart set to TRUE. If you do not call DAQmxStartTask and DAQmxStopTask when you call NI-DAQmx Read functions or NI-DAQmx Write functions multiple times, such as in a loop, the task starts and stops repeatedly. Starting and stopping a task repeatedly reduces the performance of the application.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task to stop. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

Task Configuration/Control

### DAQmxWaitUntilTaskDone

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxWaitUntilTaskDone(TaskHandle taskHandle, float64 timeToWait)

#### Remarks

Waits for the measurement or generation to complete. Use this function to [ensure that the specified operation is complete](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_waituntildone) before you stop the task.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task used in this function. |
| timeToWait | [in] | float64 | The maximum amount of time, in seconds, to wait for the measurement or generation to complete. The function returns an error if the time elapses before the measurement or generation is complete. A value of -1 (DAQmx_Val_WaitInfinitely) means to wait indefinitely. If you set timeToWait to 0, the function checks once and returns an error if the measurement or generation is not done. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

## TOPIC 01347: DAQmxClearTask

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxClearTask(TaskHandle taskHandle)RemarksClears the task. Before clearing, this function aborts the task, if necessary, and releases any resources reserved by the task. You cannot use a task once you clear the task without recreating or reloading the task. If you use the DAQmx

### DAQmxClearTask

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxClearTask(TaskHandle taskHandle)

#### Remarks

Clears the [task](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_tasksnidaqmx). Before clearing, this function aborts the task, if necessary, and releases any resources reserved by the task. You cannot use a task once you clear the task without recreating or reloading the task. If you use the DAQmxCreateTask function or any of the NI-DAQmx Create Channel functions within a loop, use this function within the loop after you finish with the task to avoid allocating unnecessary memory.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task to clear. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 01350: DAQmxTaskControl

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__task__configuration__control__advanced_1ga5b8c5e73dd4a7cbf31086ca774208fe2.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__task__configuration__control__advanced_1ga5b8c5e73dd4a7cbf31086ca774208fe2.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxTaskControl(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 action)RemarksAlters the state of a task according to the action you specify. To minimize the time required to start a task, for example, DAQmxTaskControl can commit the task prior to starting.ParametersNameDirectionTypeDescriptiontas

### DAQmxTaskControl

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxTaskControl(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 action)

#### Remarks

Alters the [state](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_taskstatemodel) of a task according to the action you specify. To minimize the time required to start a task, for example, DAQmxTaskControl can commit the task prior to starting.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task used in this function. |
| action | [in] | int32 | Specifies how to alter the task state. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_Task_StartStarts execution of the task.DAQmx_Val_Task_StopStops execution of the task.DAQmx_Val_Task_VerifyVerifies that all task parameters are valid for the hardware.DAQmx_Val_Task_CommitPrograms the hardware as much as possible according to the task configuration.DAQmx_Val_Task_ReserveReserves the hardware resources needed for the task. No other tasks can reserve these same resources.DAQmx_Val_Task_UnreserveReleases all previously reserved resources.DAQmx_Val_Task_AbortAbort is used to stop an operation, such as Read or Write, that is currently active. Abort puts the task into an unstable but recoverable state. To recover the task, call Start to restart the task or call Stop to reset the task without starting it. |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Task_Start | Starts execution of the task. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Task_Stop | Stops execution of the task. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Task_Verify | Verifies that all task parameters are valid for the hardware. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Task_Commit | Programs the hardware as much as possible according to the task configuration. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Task_Reserve | Reserves the hardware resources needed for the task. No other tasks can reserve these same resources. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Task_Unreserve | Releases all previously reserved resources. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Task_Abort | Abort is used to stop an operation, such as Read or Write, that is currently active. Abort puts the task into an unstable but recoverable state. To recover the task, call Start to restart the task or call Stop to reset the task without starting it. |  |  |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

Advanced

### DAQmxGetNthTaskDevice

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxGetNthTaskDevice(TaskHandle taskHandle, uInt32 index, char buffer[], int32 bufferSize)

#### Remarks

| --- | --- | --- | --- |

#### Returns

## TOPIC 01352: DAQmxRegisterSignalEvent

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__task__configuration__control__events_1ga3130f2dfabf47856f7c4f761fbe9bec4.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__task__configuration__control__events_1ga3130f2dfabf47856f7c4f761fbe9bec4.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxRegisterSignalEvent(TaskHandle task, int32 signalID, uInt32 options, DAQmxSignalEventCallbackPtr callbackFunction, void *callbackData)RemarksRegisters a callback function to receive an event when the specified hardware event occurs. When you stop a task explicitly any pendin

### DAQmxRegisterSignalEvent

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxRegisterSignalEvent(TaskHandle task, int32 signalID, uInt32 options, DAQmxSignalEventCallbackPtr callbackFunction, void *callbackData)

#### Remarks

Registers a callback function to receive an event when the specified [hardware event](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_events) occurs. When you stop a task explicitly any pending events are discarded. For example, if you call [DAQmxStopTask](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__task__configuration__control_1ga85d6ee7f3518c1eb26ec0f01de160392.html) then you do not receive any pending events.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| task | [in] | TaskHandle | The task used in this function. |
| signalID | [in] | int32 | The signal for which you want to receive results. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_SampleClockSample clockDAQmx_Val_SampleCompleteEventSample complete eventDAQmx_Val_ChangeDetectionEventChange detection eventDAQmx_Val_CounterOutputEventCounter output event |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_SampleClock | Sample clock |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_SampleCompleteEvent | Sample complete event |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_ChangeDetectionEvent | Change detection event |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_CounterOutputEvent | Counter output event |  |  |
| options | [in] | uInt32 | Use this parameter to set certain options. You can combine flags with the bitwise-OR operator ('\|') to set multiple options. Pass a value of zero if no options need to be set. ValueDescription0The callback function is called in a DAQmx thread. This is the default value.DAQmx_Val_SynchronousEventCallbacksThe callback function is called in the thread which registered the event. In order for the callback to occur, you must be processing messages. This option is supported only on Windows.Note If you are receiving synchronous events faster than you are processing them, then the user interface of your application might become unresponsive. |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| 0 | The callback function is called in a DAQmx thread. This is the default value. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_SynchronousEventCallbacks | The callback function is called in the thread which registered the event. In order for the callback to occur, you must be processing messages. This option is supported only on Windows. |  |  |
| Note If you are receiving synchronous events faster than you are processing them, then the user interface of your application might become unresponsive. |  |  |  |
| callbackFunction | [in] | DAQmxSignalEventCallbackPtr | The function that you want DAQmx to call when the event occurs. The function you pass in this parameter must have the following prototype: int32 CVICALLBACK Callback (TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 signalID, void *callbackData); Upon entry to the callback, the taskHandle parameter contains the handle to the task on which the event occurred. The signalID parameter contains the value you passed in the signalID parameter of this function. The callbackData parameter contains the value you passed in the callbackData parameter of this function. Passing NULL for this parameter unregisters the event callback function. |
| callbackData | [in] | void * | A value that you want DAQmx to pass to the callback function as the function data parameter. Callback functions may be called even after a task is cleared. Do not pass the address of a local variable, a variable associated with a cleared task, or any other variable that might not be valid when the function is executed. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

Events

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-c-api-ref path=group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__task__configuration__control__events_1gac007d7b1000d4bbd17da49e606d1b59d.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 01353: DAQmxRegisterDoneEvent

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__task__configuration__control__events_1gac007d7b1000d4bbd17da49e606d1b59d.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__task__configuration__control__events_1gac007d7b1000d4bbd17da49e606d1b59d.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxRegisterDoneEvent(TaskHandle task, uInt32 options, DAQmxDoneEventCallbackPtr callbackFunction, void *callbackData)RemarksRegisters a callback function to receive an event when a task stops due to an error or when a finite acquisition task or finite generation task completes

### DAQmxRegisterDoneEvent

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxRegisterDoneEvent(TaskHandle task, uInt32 options, DAQmxDoneEventCallbackPtr callbackFunction, void *callbackData)

#### Remarks

Registers a callback function to receive an event when a task stops due to an error or when a finite acquisition task or finite generation task completes execution. A Done event does not occur when a task is stopped explicitly, such as by calling [DAQmxStopTask](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__task__configuration__control_1ga85d6ee7f3518c1eb26ec0f01de160392.html).

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| task | [in] | TaskHandle | The task used in this function. |
| options | [in] | uInt32 | Use this parameter to set certain options. You can combine flags with the bitwise-OR operator ('\|') to set multiple options. Pass a value of zero if no options need to be set. ValueDescription0The callback function is called in a DAQmx thread. This is the default value.DAQmx_Val_SynchronousEventCallbacksThe callback function is called in the thread which registered the event. In order for the callback to occur, you must be processing messages. This option is supported only on Windows.Note If you are receiving synchronous events faster than you are processing them, then the user interface of your application might become unresponsive. |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| 0 | The callback function is called in a DAQmx thread. This is the default value. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_SynchronousEventCallbacks | The callback function is called in the thread which registered the event. In order for the callback to occur, you must be processing messages. This option is supported only on Windows. |  |  |
| Note If you are receiving synchronous events faster than you are processing them, then the user interface of your application might become unresponsive. |  |  |  |
| callbackFunction | [in] | DAQmxDoneEventCallbackPtr | The function that you want DAQmx to call when the event occurs. The function you pass in this parameter must have the following prototype: int32 CVICALLBACK Callback (TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 status, void *callbackData); Upon entry to the callback, the taskHandle parameter contains the handle to the task on which the event occurred. The status parameter contains the status of the task when the event occurred. If the status value is negative, it indicates an error. If the status value is zero, it indicates no error. If the status value is positive, it indicates a warning. The callbackData parameter contains the value you passed in the callbackData parameter of this function. Passing NULL for this parameter unregisters the event callback function. |
| callbackData | [in] | void * | A value that you want DAQmx to pass to the callback function as the function data parameter. Callback functions may be called even after a task is cleared. Do not pass the address of a local variable, a variable associated with a cleared task, or any other variable that might not be valid when the function is executed. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

Events

## TOPIC 01355: DAQmxCfgImplicitTiming

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__timing_1ga0c2c44433d94c1f4992a285fad557b30.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__timing_1ga0c2c44433d94c1f4992a285fad557b30.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxCfgImplicitTiming(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 sampleMode, uInt64 sampsPerChan)RemarksSets only the number of samples to acquire or generate without specifying timing. Typically, you should use this function when the task does not require sample timing, such as tasks that us

### DAQmxCfgImplicitTiming

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxCfgImplicitTiming(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 sampleMode, uInt64 sampsPerChan)

#### Remarks

Sets only the number of samples to acquire or generate without specifying timing. Typically, you should use this function when the task does not require sample timing, such as tasks that use counters for buffered frequency measurement, buffered period measurement, or pulse train generation. For finite counter output tasks, sampsPerChanToAcquire is the number of pulses to generate.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task used in this function. |
| sampleMode | [in] | int32 | Specifies whether the task acquires or generates samples continuously or if it acquires or generates a finite number of samples. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_FiniteSampsAcquire or generate a finite number of samples.DAQmx_Val_ContSampsAcquire or generate samples until you stop the task.DAQmx_Val_HWTimedSinglePointAcquire or generate samples continuously using hardware timing without a buffer. Hardware timed single point sample mode is supported only for the sample clock and change detection timing types. |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_FiniteSamps | Acquire or generate a finite number of samples. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_ContSamps | Acquire or generate samples until you stop the task. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_HWTimedSinglePoint | Acquire or generate samples continuously using hardware timing without a buffer. Hardware timed single point sample mode is supported only for the sample clock and change detection timing types. |  |  |
| sampsPerChan | [in] | uInt64 | The number of samples to acquire or generate for each channel in the task if sampleMode is DAQmx_Val_FiniteSamps. If sampleMode is DAQmx_Val_ContSamps, NI-DAQmx uses this value to determine the buffer size. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

Timing

## TOPIC 01356: DAQmxCfgBurstHandshakingTimingImportClock

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__timing_1ga60d5d5a431364d5b2db2acd787a77657.html`

- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxCfgBurstHandshakingTimingImportClock(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 sampleMode, uInt64 sampsPerChan, float64 sampleClkRate, const char sampleClkSrc[], int32 sampleClkActiveEdge, int32 pauseWhen, int32 readyEventActiveLevel)RemarksConfigures when the DAQ device transfers data t

### DAQmxCfgBurstHandshakingTimingImportClock

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxCfgBurstHandshakingTimingImportClock(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 sampleMode, uInt64 sampsPerChan, float64 sampleClkRate, const char sampleClkSrc[], int32 sampleClkActiveEdge, int32 pauseWhen, int32 readyEventActiveLevel)

#### Remarks

Configures when the DAQ device transfers data to a peripheral device, using an imported sample clock to control [burst handshaking timing](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_smpletimingtype).

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task used in this function. |
| sampleMode | [in] | int32 | Specifies whether the task acquires or generates samples continuously or if it acquires or generates a finite number of samples. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_FiniteSampsAcquire or generate a finite number of samples.DAQmx_Val_ContSampsAcquire or generate samples until you stop the task.DAQmx_Val_HWTimedSinglePointAcquire or generate samples continuously using hardware timing without a buffer. Hardware timed single point sample mode is supported only for the sample clock and change detection timing types. |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_FiniteSamps | Acquire or generate a finite number of samples. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_ContSamps | Acquire or generate samples until you stop the task. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_HWTimedSinglePoint | Acquire or generate samples continuously using hardware timing without a buffer. Hardware timed single point sample mode is supported only for the sample clock and change detection timing types. |  |  |
| sampsPerChan | [in] | uInt64 | The number of samples to acquire from each channel if sampleMode is DAQmx_Val_FiniteSamps. If sampleMode is DAQmx_Val_ContSamps, NI-DAQmx uses this value to determine the buffer size. |
| sampleClkRate | [in] | float64 | Specifies the sampling rate in samples per channel per second. If you use an external source for the Sample Clock, set this input to the maximum expected rate of that clock. |
| sampleClkSrc | [in] | const char[] | Specifies the terminal of the signal to use as the Sample Clock. |
| sampleClkActiveEdge | [in] | int32 | Specifies on which edge of a clock pulse sampling takes place. This property is useful primarily when the signal you use as the Sample Clock is not a periodic clock. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_RisingAcquire or generate samples on the rising edges of the Sample Clock.DAQmx_Val_FallingAcquire or generate samples on the falling edges of the Sample Clock. |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Rising | Acquire or generate samples on the rising edges of the Sample Clock. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Falling | Acquire or generate samples on the falling edges of the Sample Clock. |  |  |
| pauseWhen | [in] | int32 | Specifies whether the task pauses while the signal is high or low. |
| readyEventActiveLevel | [in] | int32 | Specifies the polarity for the Ready for Transfer event. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.
