## TOPIC 01359: DAQmxCfgPipelinedSampClkTiming

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__timing_1ga82119578b31ea85f6410c7037b969cc8.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__timing_1ga82119578b31ea85f6410c7037b969cc8.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxCfgPipelinedSampClkTiming(TaskHandle taskHandle, const char source[], float64 rate, int32 activeEdge, int32 sampleMode, uInt64 sampsPerChan)RemarksSets the source of the Sample Clock, the rate of the Sample Clock, and the number of samples to acquire or generate. The device

### DAQmxCfgPipelinedSampClkTiming

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxCfgPipelinedSampClkTiming(TaskHandle taskHandle, const char source[], float64 rate, int32 activeEdge, int32 sampleMode, uInt64 sampsPerChan)

#### Remarks

Sets the source of the [Sample Clock](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_sampclock), the rate of the Sample Clock, and the number of samples to acquire or generate. The device acquires or generates samples on each Sample Clock edge, but does not respond to certain triggers until a few Sample Clock edges later. Pipelining allows higher data transfer rates at the cost of increased trigger response latency. Refer to the device documentation for information about which triggers pipelining affects. This timing type allows handshaking using the Pause trigger, the Ready for Transfer event, or the Data Active event. Refer to the device documentation for more information. This timing type is supported only by the NI 6536 and NI 6537.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task used in this function. |
| source | [in] | const char[] | The source terminal of the Sample Clock. To use the internal clock of the device, use NULL or use OnboardClock. |
| rate | [in] | float64 | The sampling rate in samples per second per channel. If you use an external source for the Sample Clock, set this value to the maximum expected rate of that clock. |
| activeEdge | [in] | int32 | Specifies on which edge of the clock to acquire or generate samples. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_RisingAcquire or generate samples on the rising edges of the Sample Clock.DAQmx_Val_FallingAcquire or generate samples on the falling edges of the Sample Clock. |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Rising | Acquire or generate samples on the rising edges of the Sample Clock. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_Falling | Acquire or generate samples on the falling edges of the Sample Clock. |  |  |
| sampleMode | [in] | int32 | Specifies whether the task acquires or generates samples continuously or if it acquires or generates a finite number of samples. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_FiniteSampsAcquire or generate a finite number of samples.DAQmx_Val_ContSampsAcquire or generate samples until you stop the task.DAQmx_Val_HWTimedSinglePointAcquire or generate samples continuously using hardware timing without a buffer. Hardware timed single point sample mode is supported only for the sample clock and change detection timing types. |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_FiniteSamps | Acquire or generate a finite number of samples. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_ContSamps | Acquire or generate samples until you stop the task. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_HWTimedSinglePoint | Acquire or generate samples continuously using hardware timing without a buffer. Hardware timed single point sample mode is supported only for the sample clock and change detection timing types. |  |  |
| sampsPerChan | [in] | uInt64 | The number of samples to acquire or generate for each channel in the task if sampleMode is DAQmx_Val_FiniteSamps. If sampleMode is DAQmx_Val_ContSamps, NI-DAQmx uses this value to determine the buffer size. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

Timing

## TOPIC 01364: DAQmxCfgAnlgMultiEdgeRefTrig

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__triggering__reference__trigger_1ga76cbe7ca9891682a958256127ddb9f3b.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__triggering__reference__trigger_1ga76cbe7ca9891682a958256127ddb9f3b.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxCfgAnlgMultiEdgeRefTrig(TaskHandle taskHandle, const char triggerSources[], const int32 triggerSlopeArray[], const float64 triggerLevelArray[], uInt32 pretriggerSamples, uInt32 arraySize)RemarksConfigures the task to stop the acquisition when the device acquires all pretrigg

### DAQmxCfgAnlgMultiEdgeRefTrig

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxCfgAnlgMultiEdgeRefTrig(TaskHandle taskHandle, const char triggerSources[], const int32 triggerSlopeArray[], const float64 triggerLevelArray[], uInt32 pretriggerSamples, uInt32 arraySize)

#### Remarks

Configures the task to stop the acquisition when the device acquires all pretrigger samples, any of the configured analog signals reaches the levels you specify, and the device acquires all post-trigger samples. Multi-edge triggering treats the specified triggers as if a logical OR is applied.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task used in this function. |
| triggerSources | [in] | const char[] | A comma-separated string specifying a list of terminals, physical channel names, or ranges of physical channels where there are an analog signals to use as the sources of the trigger. |
| triggerSlopeArray | [in] | const int32[] | The array containing the slopes of the signals to start acquiring or generating samples when the respective signal crosses the specified trigger level. Each element of the array corresponds to the sources specified in triggerSources and triggerLevelArray. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_RisingSlopeTrigger on the rising slope of the signal.DAQmx_Val_FallingSlopeTrigger on the falling slope of the signal. |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_RisingSlope | Trigger on the rising slope of the signal. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_FallingSlope | Trigger on the falling slope of the signal. |  |  |
| triggerLevelArray | [in] | const float64[] | The array containing the thresholds at which to start acquiring or generating samples. Each element of the array corresponds to the sources specified in triggerSources and triggerSlopeArray. Specify these values in the units of the measurement or generation. Use the triggerSlopeArray to specify on which slopes to trigger at the respective thresholds. |
| pretriggerSamples | [in] | uInt32 | The minimum number of samples per channel to acquire before recognizing the Reference Trigger. The number of posttrigger samples per channel is equal to number of samples per channel in the NI-DAQmx Timing functions minus pretriggerSamples. |
| arraySize | [in] | uInt32 | The size of triggerSlopeArray and triggerLevelArray. This must correspond to the number of sources specified in triggerSources. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

Reference Trigger

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-c-api-ref path=group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__triggering__reference__trigger_1ga901d1c8dd45e74ba3c9b27a7508068ea.html language=enus -->

### DAQmxCfgAnlgWindowRefTrig

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxCfgAnlgWindowRefTrig(TaskHandle taskHandle, const char triggerSource[], int32 triggerWhen, float64 windowTop, float64 windowBottom, uInt32 pretriggerSamples)

#### Remarks

Configures the task to stop the acquisition when the device acquires all pretrigger samples, an analog signal enters or leaves a range you specify, and the device acquires all post-trigger samples.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task used in this function. |
| triggerSource | [in] | const char[] | The name of a virtual channel or terminal where there is an analog signal to use as the source of the trigger. For E Series devices, if you use a virtual channel, it must be the only channel in the task. The only terminal you can use for E Series devices is PFI0. |
| triggerWhen | [in] | int32 | Specifies whether the Reference Trigger occurs when the signal enters the window or when it leaves the window. Use windowBottom and windowTop to specify the limits of the window. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_EnteringWinTrigger when the signal enters the window.DAQmx_Val_LeavingWinTrigger when the signal leaves the window. |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_EnteringWin | Trigger when the signal enters the window. |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_LeavingWin | Trigger when the signal leaves the window. |  |  |
| windowTop | [in] | float64 | The upper limit of the window. Specify this value in the units of the measurement or generation. |
| windowBottom | [in] | float64 | The lower limit of the window. Specify this value in the units of the measurement or generation. |
| pretriggerSamples | [in] | uInt32 | The minimum number of samples per channel to acquire before recognizing the Reference Trigger. The number of posttrigger samples per channel is equal to number of samples per channel in the NI-DAQmx Timing functions minus pretriggerSamples. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

Reference Trigger

## TOPIC 01374: DAQmxWriteDigitalU16

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__write__functions_1ga106579448fc06cb424fbaf095e168975.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__write__functions_1ga106579448fc06cb424fbaf095e168975.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxWriteDigitalU16(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, bool32 autoStart, float64 timeout, bool32 dataLayout, const uInt16 writeArray[], int32 *sampsPerChanWritten, bool32 *reserved)RemarksWrites multiple 16-bit unsigned integer samples to a task that contains one or m

### DAQmxWriteDigitalU16

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxWriteDigitalU16(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, bool32 autoStart, float64 timeout, bool32 dataLayout, const uInt16 writeArray[], int32 *sampsPerChanWritten, bool32 *reserved)

#### Remarks

Writes multiple 16-bit unsigned [integer samples](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_digitaldata) to a task that contains one or more [digital output channels](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_virtchantypes). Use this format for devices with up to 16 lines per port.

Note

If you configured timing for your task, your write is considered a buffered write. Buffered writes require a minimum buffer size of two samples. If you do not configure the buffer size using DAQmxCfgOutputBuffer, NI-DAQmx automatically configures the buffer when you configure sample timing. If you attempt to write one sample for a buffered write without configuring the buffer, you will receive an error.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task to write samples to. |
| numSampsPerChan | [in] | int32 | The number of samples, per channel, to write. You must pass in a value of 0 or more in order for the sample to write. If you pass a negative number, this function returns an error. |
| autoStart | [in] | bool32 | Specifies whether or not this function automatically starts the task if you do not start it. |
| timeout | [in] | float64 | The amount of time, in seconds, to wait for this function to write all the samples. To specify an infinite wait, pass -1 (DAQmx_Val_WaitInfinitely). This function returns an error if the timeout elapses. A value of 0 indicates to try once to write the submitted samples. If this function successfully writes all submitted samples, it does not return an error. Otherwise, the function returns a timeout error and returns the number of samples actually written. |
| dataLayout | [in] | bool32 | Specifies how the samples are arranged, either interleaved or noninterleaved. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_GroupByChannelGroup by channel (noninterleaved)DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumberGroup by sample (interleaved) |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByChannel | Group by channel (noninterleaved) |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumber | Group by sample (interleaved) |  |  |
| writeArray | [in] | const uInt16[] | The array of 16-bit integer samples to write to the task. |
| reserved | [in] | bool32 * | Reserved for future use. Pass NULL to this parameter. |
| sampsPerChanWritten | [out] | int32 * | The actual number of samples per channel successfully written to the buffer. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

Write Functions

### DAQmxWriteDigitalScalarU32

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxWriteDigitalScalarU32(TaskHandle taskHandle, bool32 autoStart, float64 timeout, uInt32 value, bool32 *reserved)

Otherwise, the function returns a timeout error. |
| value | [in] | uInt32 | A 32-bit integer sample to write to the task. |
| reserved | [in] | bool32 * | Reserved for future use. Pass NULL to this parameter. |

## TOPIC 01376: DAQmxWriteBinaryI16

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__write__functions_1ga21c6eb375a1f350500d77585b69e2093.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__write__functions_1ga21c6eb375a1f350500d77585b69e2093.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxWriteBinaryI16(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, bool32 autoStart, float64 timeout, bool32 dataLayout, const int16 writeArray[], int32 *sampsPerChanWritten, bool32 *reserved)RemarksWrites unscaled signed integer samples to the task.If you configured timing for yo

### DAQmxWriteBinaryI16

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxWriteBinaryI16(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, bool32 autoStart, float64 timeout, bool32 dataLayout, const int16 writeArray[], int32 *sampsPerChanWritten, bool32 *reserved)

#### Remarks

Writes [unscaled](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_unscaleddata) signed integer samples to the task.

Note

If you configured timing for your task, your write is considered a buffered write. Buffered writes require a minimum buffer size of 2 samples. If you do not configure the buffer size using DAQmxCfgOutputBuffer, NI-DAQmx automatically configures the buffer when you configure sample timing. If you attempt to write one sample for a buffered write without configuring the buffer, you will receive an error.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task to write samples to. |
| numSampsPerChan | [in] | int32 | The number of samples, per channel, to write. You must pass in a value of 0 or more in order for the sample to write. If you pass a negative number, this function returns an error. |
| autoStart | [in] | bool32 | Specifies whether or not this function automatically starts the task if you do not start it. |
| timeout | [in] | float64 | The amount of time, in seconds, to wait for this function to write all the samples. To specify an infinite wait, pass -1 (DAQmx_Val_WaitInfinitely). This function returns an error if the timeout elapses. A value of 0 indicates to try once to write the submitted samples. If this function successfully writes all submitted samples, it does not return an error. Otherwise, the function returns a timeout error and returns the number of samples actually written. |
| dataLayout | [in] | bool32 | Specifies how the samples are arranged, either interleaved or noninterleaved. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_GroupByChannelGroup by channel (noninterleaved)DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumberGroup by sample (interleaved) |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByChannel | Group by channel (noninterleaved) |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumber | Group by sample (interleaved) |  |  |
| writeArray | [in] | const int16[] | The array of 16-bit samples to write to the task. |
| reserved | [in] | bool32 * | Reserved for future use. Pass NULL to this parameter. |
| sampsPerChanWritten | [out] | int32 * | The actual number of samples per channel successfully written to the buffer. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 01377: DAQmxWriteCtrFreq

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__write__functions_1ga25d3c593682914ae8f2803c03c3c3bbb.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__write__functions_1ga25d3c593682914ae8f2803c03c3c3bbb.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntaxint32 __CFUNC DAQmxWriteCtrFreq(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, bool32 autoStart, float64 timeout, bool32 dataLayout, const float64 frequency[], const float64 dutyCycle[], int32 *numSampsPerChanWritten, bool32 *reserved)RemarksWrites a new pulse frequency and duty cycle to each c

### DAQmxWriteCtrFreq

#### Syntax

int32 __CFUNC DAQmxWriteCtrFreq(TaskHandle taskHandle, int32 numSampsPerChan, bool32 autoStart, float64 timeout, bool32 dataLayout, const float64 frequency[], const float64 dutyCycle[], int32 *numSampsPerChanWritten, bool32 *reserved)

#### Remarks

Writes a new pulse frequency and duty cycle to each channel in a continuous counter output task that contains one or more channels.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| taskHandle | [in] | TaskHandle | The task to write samples to. |
| numSampsPerChan | [in] | int32 | The number of samples, per channel, to write. You must pass in a value of 0 or more in order for the sample to write. If you pass a negative number, this function returns an error. |
| autoStart | [in] | bool32 | Specifies whether or not this function automatically starts the task if you do not start it. |
| timeout | [in] | float64 | The amount of time, in seconds, to wait for this function to write all the samples. To specify an infinite wait, pass -1 (DAQmx_Val_WaitInfinitely). This function returns an error if the timeout elapses. A value of 0 indicates to try once to write the submitted samples. If this function successfully writes all submitted samples, it does not return an error. Otherwise, the function returns a timeout error and returns the number of samples actually written. |
| dataLayout | [in] | bool32 | Specifies how the samples are arranged, either interleaved or noninterleaved. ValueDescriptionDAQmx_Val_GroupByChannelGroup by channel (noninterleaved)DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumberGroup by sample (interleaved) |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByChannel | Group by channel (noninterleaved) |  |  |
| DAQmx_Val_GroupByScanNumber | Group by sample (interleaved) |  |  |
| frequency | [in] | const float64[] | Specifies at what frequency to generate pulses. |
| dutyCycle | [in] | const float64[] | The width of the pulse divided by the pulse period. NI-DAQmx uses this ratio, combined with frequency, to determine both pulse width and pulse delay. |
| reserved | [in] | bool32 * | Reserved for future use. Pass NULL to this parameter. |
| numSampsPerChanWritten | [out] | int32 * | The actual number of samples per channel successfully written to the buffer. |

#### Returns

The error code returned by the function in the event of an error or warning. A value of 0 indicates success. A positive value indicates a warning. A negative value indicates an error.

Parent topic:

Zero indicates to allocate no buffer. Use a buffer size of 0 to perform a hardware-timed operation without using a buffer. Setting this

### DAQmx_Buf_Output_BufSize

#### Syntax

DAQmx_Buf_Output_BufSize

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| uInt32 | Specifies the number of samples the output buffer can hold for each channel in the task. Zero indicates to allocate no buffer. Use a buffer size of 0 to perform a hardware-timed operation without using a buffer. Setting this property overrides the automatic output buffer allocation that NI-DAQmx performs. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetBufOutputBufSize](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga3b1c6fcef9e890e67aa7a9bab5aec2cc.html)

### DAQmx_AI_Accel_Units

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AI_Accel_Units

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the units to use to return acceleration measurements from the channel. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_AccelUnit_g | 10186 | 1 g is approximately equal to 9.81 m/s/s. |
| DAQmx_Val_MetersPerSecondSquared | 12470 | Meters per second per second. |
| DAQmx_Val_InchesPerSecondSquared | 12471 | Inches per second per second. |
| DAQmx_Val_FromCustomScale | 10065 | Units a custom scale specifies. If you select this value, you must specify a custom scale name. |

### DAQmx_AI_Bridge_Units

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AI_Bridge_Units

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies in which unit to return voltage ratios from the channel. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |

| DAQmx_Val_mVoltsPerVolt | 15897 | Millivolts per volt. |
| DAQmx_Val_FromCustomScale | 10065 | Units a custom scale specifies. If you select this value, you must specify a custom scale name. |
| DAQmx_Val_FromTEDS | 12516 | Units defined by TEDS information associated with the channel. |

## TOPIC 01409: DAQmx_AI_Bridge_ScaleType

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__analog__input__bridge__scaling__parameters_1ga573b83fbce3e5de9b5db530384736fe0.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__analog__input__bridge__scaling__parameters_1ga573b83fbce3e5de9b5db530384736fe0.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_AI_Bridge_ScaleTypeRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies the scaling type to use when scaling electrical values from the sensor to physical units.Valid valuesDAQmx_Val_None10230Do not scale electrical values to physical units.DAQmx_Val_TwoPointLinear15898You provide two p

### DAQmx_AI_Bridge_ScaleType

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AI_Bridge_ScaleType

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the scaling type to use when scaling electrical values from the sensor to physical units. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_None | 10230 | Do not scale electrical values to physical units. |
| DAQmx_Val_TwoPointLinear | 15898 | You provide two pairs of electrical values and their corresponding physical values. NI-DAQmx uses those values to calculate the slope and y-intercept of a linear equation and uses that equation to scale electrical values to physical values. |
| DAQmx_Val_Table | 10450 | Map an array of electrical values to an array of corresponding physical values, with all other values scaled proportionally. If you specify this scaling type, Maximum Value and Minimum Value must be within the smallest and largest physical values. For any data outside those endpoints, NI-DAQmx coerces that data to the endpoints. |
| DAQmx_Val_Polynomial | 10449 | Scale values by using an Nth order polynomial equation. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetAIBridgeScaleType](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga82669c9af7da6eb861d773d0948121b0.html)
- [DAQmxSetAIBridgeScaleType](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga653bacd19a96f19d09cb904adad3b101.html)
- [DAQmxResetAIBridgeScaleType](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga950faf3e59abfbb2adca3a7eb2c0fcb1.html)

Parent topic:

### DAQmx_AI_Bridge_Poly_ReverseCoeff

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AI_Bridge_Poly_ReverseCoeff

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64* | Specifies an array of coefficients for the polynomial that converts physical values to electrical values. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. For example, if index three of the array is 9, the fourth term of the equation is 9x^3. |  |

- [DAQmxGetAIBridgePolyReverseCoeff](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga903066aead895f34ac8b3f99e9b43bbb.html)

Data transfers take place independently from the application.DAQmx_Val_Interrupts10204Data transfers take place independently fro

### DAQmx_AI_DataXferMech

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AI_DataXferMech

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the data transfer mode for the device. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_DMA | 10054 | Direct Memory Access. Data transfers take place independently from the application. |
| DAQmx_Val_Interrupts | 10204 | Data transfers take place independently from the application. Using interrupts increases CPU usage because the CPU must service interrupt requests. Typically, you should use interrupts if the device is out of DMA channels. |
| DAQmx_Val_ProgrammedIO | 10264 | Data transfers take place when you call an NI-DAQmx Read function or an NI-DAQmx Write function. |
| DAQmx_Val_USBbulk | 12590 | Data transfers take place independently from the application using a USB bulk pipe. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetAIDataXferMech](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gab4cd14cb540e497c516afc88ff452df8.html)
- [DAQmxSetAIDataXferMech](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga5b59b77509f0449a857c27f34bb5e2e3.html)
- [DAQmxResetAIDataXferMech](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga39abb735e8b1863c0bf09856fe68b51f.html)

- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_AI_DevScalingCoeffRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsfloat64*Indicates the coefficients of a polynomial equation that NI-DAQmx uses to scale values from the native format of the device to volts. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. For example, if index tw

### DAQmx_AI_DevScalingCoeff

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AI_DevScalingCoeff

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64* | Indicates the coefficients of a polynomial equation that NI-DAQmx uses to scale values from the native format of the device to volts. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. For example, if index two of the array is 4, the third term of the equation is 4x^2. Scaling coefficients do not account for any custom scales or sensors contained by the channel. | Not Settable |

You can get this property using:

- [DAQmxGetAIDevScalingCoeff](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga7f0c6acd3a9153e9e6b5d175f30f7a5d.html)

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__analog__input__general__properties__advanced__input__limits__fault__detection_1ga1af877cd4f4059b9b36ac4b8f672f54f.html`

- page_type: `leaf`

- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_AI_InputLimitsFaultDetect_LowerLimitRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsfloat64Specifies the level of the lower limit for input limits detection. An input sample outside the upper and lower bounds causes a fault. Note: Fault detection applies to both positive and negative inputs. For

### DAQmx_AI_InputLimitsFaultDetect_LowerLimit

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AI_InputLimitsFaultDetect_LowerLimit

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64 | Specifies the level of the lower limit for input limits detection. An input sample outside the upper and lower bounds causes a fault. Note: Fault detection applies to both positive and negative inputs. For instance, if you specify a lower limit of 2 mA and an upper limit of 12 mA, NI-DAQmx detects a fault at 15 mA and -15 mA, but not at -6 mA because it is in the range of -12 mA to -2 mA. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetAIInputLimitsFaultDetectLowerLimit](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga726c0a1e6fa2767b96c6b2f336b7e075.html)
- [DAQmxSetAIInputLimitsFaultDetectLowerLimit](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga243a80895ba8ea82601dbfa8f484f2ac.html)
- [DAQmxResetAIInputLimitsFaultDetectLowerLimit](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1gaa8b7ac1f67a8d79b0ee892fd868eda77.html)

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 01456: DAQmx_AI_SampAndHold_Enable

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__analog__input__general__properties__advanced__range_1ga55a18edd578703bb503991c05a5d59e5.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__analog__input__general__properties__advanced__range_1ga55a18edd578703bb503991c05a5d59e5.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_AI_SampAndHold_EnableRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsbool32Specifies whether to enable the sample and hold circuitry of the device. When you disable sample and hold circuitry, a small voltage offset might be introduced into the signal. You can eliminate this offset by using Auto Z

### DAQmx_AI_SampAndHold_Enable

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AI_SampAndHold_Enable

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| bool32 | Specifies whether to enable the sample and hold circuitry of the device. When you disable sample and hold circuitry, a small voltage offset might be introduced into the signal. You can eliminate this offset by using Auto Zero Mode to perform an auto zero on the channel. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetAISampAndHoldEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga0241087fd5b6ad5cc0d2d9f133eed7d4.html)
- [DAQmxSetAISampAndHoldEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga6cc65c964ec5784c4c6b557b53c12f13.html)
- [DAQmxResetAISampAndHoldEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1gad36f63e57d0b24d4e93b3b8aa74b9046.html)

| DAQmx_Val_Polynomial | 10449 | Scale values by using an Nth order polynomial equation. |
| DAQmx_Val_Table | 10450 | Map an array of prescaled values to an array of corresponding scaled values, with all other values scaled proportionally. |
| DAQmx_Val_None | 10230 |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetAIChanCalScaleType](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga3d61e68595c936e6019fd3173ee6d3eb.html)

## TOPIC 01475: DAQmx_AI_ADCTimingMode

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__analog__input__general__properties__digitizer__adc_1ga3a3ee40dc83419eeae7520eeb280f4d7.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__analog__input__general__properties__digitizer__adc_1ga3a3ee40dc83419eeae7520eeb280f4d7.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_AI_ADCTimingModeRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies the ADC timing mode, controlling the tradeoff between speed and effective resolution. Some ADC timing modes provide increased powerline noise rejection. On devices that have an AI Convert clock, this setting affects bo

### DAQmx_AI_ADCTimingMode

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AI_ADCTimingMode

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the ADC timing mode, controlling the tradeoff between speed and effective resolution. Some ADC timing modes provide increased powerline noise rejection. On devices that have an AI Convert clock, this setting affects both the maximum and default values for Rate. You must use the same ADC timing mode for all channels on a device, but you can use different ADC timing modes for different devices in the same task. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_Automatic | 16097 | Uses the most appropriate supported timing mode based on the Sample Clock Rate. |
| DAQmx_Val_HighResolution | 10195 | Increases resolution and noise rejection while decreasing conversion rate. |
| DAQmx_Val_HighSpeed | 14712 | Increases conversion rate while decreasing resolution. |
| DAQmx_Val_Best50HzRejection | 14713 | Improves 50 Hz noise rejection while decreasing noise rejection at other frequencies. |
| DAQmx_Val_Best60HzRejection | 14714 | Improves 60 Hz noise rejection while decreasing noise rejection at other frequencies. |
| DAQmx_Val_Custom | 10137 | Use Custom Timing Mode to specify a custom value controlling the tradeoff between speed and resolution. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetAIADCTimingMode](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga9f2da0633a975017183113cc2a008896.html)
- [DAQmxSetAIADCTimingMode](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gabe2846956e2302ce1b804e186fdeed1d.html)
- [DAQmxResetAIADCTimingMode](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga5d033c5db0b17fe4b1403e322150a1ea.html)

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 01483: DAQmx_AI_Lowpass_SwitchCap_ExtClkFreq

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__analog__input__general__properties__filter__analog__fil2229066decb682018d2c6617c0f622d5_1gad4b713eb3808dea519428c9a582083e7.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__analog__input__general__properties__filter__analog__fil2229066decb682018d2c6617c0f622d5_1gad4b713eb3808dea519428c9a582083e7.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_AI_Lowpass_SwitchCap_ExtClkFreqRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsfloat64Specifies the frequency of the external clock when you set Clock Source to DAQmx_Val_External. NI-DAQmx uses this frequency to set the pre- and post- filters on the SCXI-1141, SCXI-1142, and SCXI-1143. On those

### DAQmx_AI_Lowpass_SwitchCap_ExtClkFreq

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AI_Lowpass_SwitchCap_ExtClkFreq

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64 | Specifies the frequency of the external clock when you set Clock Source to DAQmx_Val_External. NI-DAQmx uses this frequency to set the pre- and post- filters on the SCXI-1141, SCXI-1142, and SCXI-1143. On those devices, NI-DAQmx determines the filter cutoff by using the equation f/(100*n), where f is the external frequency, and n is the external clock divisor. Refer to the SCXI-1141/1142/1143 User Manual for more information. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetAILowpassSwitchCapExtClkFreq](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga9e6f3edb1f1d5b0cf6b63af6c5cec055.html)
- [DAQmxSetAILowpassSwitchCapExtClkFreq](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gaebcec00273e15434da7e007bc7ab4a72.html)
- [DAQmxResetAILowpassSwitchCapExtClkFreq](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga9e29d371ffc34ff09d706eda35b3268d.html)

Parent topic:

### DAQmx_AI_FilterDelayAdjustment

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AI_FilterDelayAdjustment

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64 | Specifies the amount of filter delay that gets removed if Remove Filter Delay is enabled. This delay adjustment is in addition to the value indicated by Filter Delay. This delay adjustment is in the units you specify with Filter Delay Units. |  |
